<p>The men's tournament in <a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">basketball</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2016_Summer_Olympics" title="2016 Summer Olympics">2016 Olympic Games</a> in <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a> began on 6 August and ended on 21 August.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-drawresults_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-drawresults-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p>The gold medal game in this discipline was the final competitive event before the Closing Ceremony.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup></p>
<p>The United States won their fifteenth gold medal after defeating Serbia 96–66 in the <a href="#Gold_medal_game">gold medal match</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> the largest margin of victory in a gold medal game since the <a href="/wiki/Basketball_at_the_1992_Summer_Olympics" title="Basketball at the 1992 Summer Olympics">1992 Olympics</a>. Spain won the bronze medal after a <a href="#Bronze_medal_game">89–88 win</a> over Australia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Squads">Squads</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Basketball_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Squads">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Basketball_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_team_rosters" title="Basketball at the 2016 Summer Olympics – Men's team rosters">Basketball at the 2016 Summer Olympics – Men's team rosters</a></div>
<p>Each NOC was limited to one team per tournament. Each team had a roster of twelve players, one of which could be a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Naturalized" title="Naturalized">naturalized</a> player.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Referees">Referees</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Basketball_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Referees">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The following referees were selected for the tournament.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup></p>
<div class="div-col columns column-count column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2;">
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Angola" title="Angola"><img alt="Angola" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Flag_of_Angola.svg/23px-Flag_of_Angola.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Flag_of_Angola.svg/35px-Flag_of_Angola.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9d/Flag_of_Angola.svg/45px-Flag_of_Angola.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> Carlos Júlio</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina"><img alt="Argentina" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> Leandro Lezcano</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Draw">Draw</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Basketball_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Draw">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The draw was held at the FIBA Headquarters, also known as the "House of Basketball" in <a href="/wiki/Mies" title="Mies">Mies</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a> on 11 March 2016. As the three winners of the <a href="/wiki/2016_FIBA_World_Olympic_Qualifying_Tournaments_for_Men" title="2016 FIBA World Olympic Qualifying Tournaments for Men">2016 FIBA World Olympic Qualifying Tournaments for Men</a> (OQT) were yet to be known, they were assigned placeholders as "OQT 1", "OQT 2" and "OQT 3". These were the pot assignments:</p>

<p>OQT 2<br/>
OQT 3</p>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>Group A was assigned with OQT 1 and OQT 2, while Group B had OQT 3.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup></p>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/2016_FIBA_World_Olympic_Qualifying_Tournament_%E2%80%93_Manila" title="2016 FIBA World Olympic Qualifying Tournament – Manila">World Olympic Qualifying Tournament</a> on 10 July 2016, another draw was held at the <a href="/wiki/Mall_of_Asia_Arena" title="Mall of Asia Arena">Mall of Asia Arena</a> in <a href="/wiki/Pasay" title="Pasay">Pasay</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>, to determine which among the teams would be assigned to which group. This was a straight draw: there were two pots containing three balls each. One pot had the names of the teams that won the Olympic Qualifying Tournaments (OQT), while the other pot had the name of the placeholders.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_ranking">Final ranking</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Basketball_at_the_2016_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Final ranking">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Rankings are determined by:</p>
<ul>
<li>1st–4th
<ul>
<li>Results of gold and bronze medal games.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>5th–8th:
<ul>
<li>Win-loss record in the preliminary round group</li>
<li>Standings in the preliminary round group (i.e. Group A's #3 is ranked higher than Group B's #4.)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>9th–10th and 11th–12th:
<ul>
<li>5th placers in the preliminary round groups are classified 9th–10th; 6th placers classified 11th–12th</li>
<li>Win-loss record in the preliminary round group</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<li><b><a href="/wiki/Basketball_at_the_2008_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Basketball at the 2008 Summer Olympics – Men's tournament">2008</a>:</b> <img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="650" data-file-width="1235" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/22px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/33px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/44px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" width="22"/> <a href="/wiki/2008_United_States_men%27s_Olympic_basketball_team" title="2008 United States men's Olympic basketball team">United States</a> <span style="font-size:90%;">(<a href="/wiki/United_States_at_the_2008_Summer_Olympics" title="United States at the 2008 Summer Olympics">USA</a>)</span></li>
